Electrostatic Interactions: Charged hosts (e.g., functionalized macrocycles) can interact with oppositely charged guests, making this mechanism particularly useful for sensing ionic species.\n\n3. π-π Stacking: Aromatic hosts (e.g., cucurbiturils, pillararenes) can engage in π-π stacking with aromatic guest molecules or indicators, providing another mode of selective binding.\n\n4. Electrostatic Interactions: Charged hosts (e.g., functionalized macrocycles) can interact with oppositely charged guests, making this mechanism particularly useful for sensing ionic species.\n\n3. π-π Stacking: Aromatic hosts (e.g., cucurbiturils, pillararenes) can engage in π-π stacking with aromatic guest molecules or indicators, providing another mode of selective binding.\n\n4.
